### FetchBannerTypesAPI<br>
**Description**: <br>
**Response Time**: 518ms <br>
**Endpoint**: [https://qa.omnycomm.com:8028/dealshub/fetch-banner-types/](https://qa.omnycomm.com:8028/dealshub/fetch-banner-types/)<br>
**Type**: POST <br>
```json
Request:
{
    "locationGroupUuid": "4724a505-8b23-45fe-bf98-4d4b23817aa4",
    "websiteGroupName": "shopnesto"
}
Response:
{
    "bannerTypes": [
        {
            "limit": 6,
            "name": "CategoryGridBanner",
            "type": "CategoryGridBanner"
        },
        {
            "limit": 1,
            "name": "FullBannerAd",
            "type": "FullBannerAd"
        },
        {
            "limit": 6,
            "name": "DealsBanner",
            "type": "DealsBanner"
        },
        {
            "limit": 5,
            "name": "HomePageSchedular",
            "type": "HomePageSchedular"
        },
        {
            "limit": 1,
            "name": "usp",
            "type": "usp"
        },
        {
            "limit": 5,
            "name": "FiveStyleBanner",
            "type": "FiveStyleBanner"
        }
    ],
    "status": 200
}
```

### UnpublishBannerAPI<br>
**Description**: <br>
**Response Time**: 256ms <br>
**Endpoint**: [https://qa.omnycomm.com:8028/dealshub/unpublish-banner/](https://qa.omnycomm.com:8028/dealshub/unpublish-banner/)<br>
**Type**: POST <br>
```json
Request:
{
    "uuid": "a4ef7083-e5cc-457b-beb8-9cb4055c5405"
}
Response:
{
    "status": 200,
    "uuid": "a4ef7083-e5cc-457b-beb8-9cb4055c5405"
}
```

### SearchSectionProductsAutocompleteAPI<br>
**Description**: <br>
**Response Time**: 295ms <br>
**Endpoint**: [https://qa.omnycomm.com:8028/dealshub/search-section-products-autocomplete/](https://qa.omnycomm.com:8028/dealshub/search-section-products-autocomplete/)<br>
**Type**: POST <br>
```json
Request:
{
    "locationGroupUuid": "4724a505-8b23-45fe-bf98-4d4b23817aa4",
    "searchString": "a",
    "sectionUuid": "38816b7d-7645-4dc6-9d91-262ca3ba535f",
    "type": "Banner",
    "websiteGroupName": "shopnesto"
}
```

**Type**: POST <br>
```json
Request:
```
```json
form-data or {}
```

```json
    "filepath": "http://cdn.omnycomm.com.s3.amazonaws.com/tmp/temp-section_9B7AVOl.xlsx",
```

### FetchLocationGroupListAPI<br>
**Description**: <br>
**Response Time**: 438ms <br>
**Endpoint**: [https://qa.omnycomm.com:8028/fetch-location-group-list/](https://qa.omnycomm.com:8028/fetch-location-group-list/)<br>
**Type**: POST <br>
```json
Request:

Response:
{
    "location_group_list": [
```

**Response Time**: 338ms <br>

**Type**: POST <br>
```json
Request:

    "orderUuid": "10cc6912-f666-487c-9864-7bc9e3d6ad88",

}

        ],

        "price": 90.0,
```

### SaveCompanyProfileAPI<br>
**Description**: <br>
**Response Time**: 275ms <br>
**Endpoint**: [https://qa.omnycomm.com:8028/save-company-profile/](https://qa.omnycomm.com:8028/save-company-profile/)<br>
**Type**: POST <br>
```json
Request:
{
    "company_data": {
        "address": "address",
        "color_scheme": {
            "add_to_cart_button_color": "#000000",
            "buy_now_button_color": "#D42512",
            "inquire_button_color": "#1EADD8",
```
